(storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/TransactionIndex.java) tracks aborted transactions for each segment\\n- LazyIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LazyIndex.java) provides lazy loading/memory mapping of indices for performance\\n\\n**Configuration and Validation:**\\n- LogConfig (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogSegment.java) represents a single log segment containing log records and associated index files\\n- LogSegments (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogSegments.java) manages a thread-safe navigable map of LogSegment instances\\n\\n**Index Files:**\\n- AbstractIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/AbstractIndex.java) is the base class providing entry format agnostic methods for all index implementations\\n- OffsetIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/OffsetIndex.java) implements a sparse index mapping offsets to physical file locations (4-byte relative offset + 4-byte file position)\\n- TimeIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/TimeIndex.java) implements timestamp-to-offset mapping (8-byte timestamp + 4-byte relative offset)\\n- TransactionIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/TransactionIndex.java) tracks aborted transactions for each segment\\n- LazyIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LazyIndex.java) provides lazy loading/memory mapping of indices for performance\\n\\n**Configuration and Validation:**\\n- LogConfig (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogConfig.java) handles all log configuration with validation including compression type, retention policies, index settings, and timestamp type\\n- LogFileUtils (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogFileUtils.java) provides utilities for log file naming with standard suffixes (.log, .index, .timeindex, .txnindex, .snapshot)\\n\\n**Log Recovery on Startup:**\\n- LogLoader (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogLoader.java) handles recovery on startup, loading segments from disk and restoring state from checkpoints\\n- ProducerStateManager (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/ProducerStateManager.java) maintains producer state and recovers from snapshot files with CRC32C validation\\n- LeaderEpochFileCache (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/epoch/LeaderEpochFileCache.java) manages leader epoch mappings and recovers from LeaderEpochCheckpointFile\\n\\n**Checkpoint Files (State Persistence):**\\n- OffsetCheckpointFile (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/OffsetCheckpointFile.java) stores offset checkpoints for log start offset and recovery point\\n- OffsetCheckpoints (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/OffsetCheckpoints.java) interface for offset checkpoint operations\\n- LeaderEpochCheckpointFile (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/LeaderEpochCheckpointFile.java) stores leader epoch information for failure recovery\\n- PartitionMetadataFile (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/PartitionMetadataFile.java) stores partition metadata including topic UUID\\n- CheckpointFile (server-common/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/common/CheckpointFile.java) is the generic checkpoint utility used by multiple checkpoint implementations\\n- CheckpointFileWithFailureHandler (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/CheckpointFileWithFailureHandler.java) wraps checkpoint files with error handling\\n- CleanShutdownFileHandler (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/CleanShutdownFileHandler.java) handles clean shutdown indicator files\\n\\n**Log Abstraction Layers:**\\n- LocalLog (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LocalLog.java) provides local storage-specific log operations\\n- UnifiedLog (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/UnifiedLog.java) is the main unified log interface supporting both local and remote storage\\n\\nThe recovery process during startup reads offset checkpoints and recovery point checkpoints, reconstructs LogSegments from disk files, recovers producer state from snapshot files with validation, and restores leader epoch information from checkpoint files. Index files are rebuilt if corrupted or missing.\"\n}\n","numLines":51,"startLine":1,"totalLines":51}}}
